</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	Dividend Yield:&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company has never declared or paid any cash dividends and does not plan to pay cash dividends in the foreseeable future, and, therefore, used an expected dividend yield of zero in the valuation model.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
<BR>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	Forfeitures:&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;As we do not have sufficient historical information to develop reasonable expectations about forfeitures, we currently apply actual forfeitures.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
<BR>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
<B>
	16. Discontinued Operations
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
<BR>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	Due to ongoing losses, the Company decided to exit its Media business. This strategic shift is intended to allow the Company to focus on its core Enterprise digital signage business and is expected to improve the Company&#146;s overall margins and profitability. The Company exited these operations on July 1, 2015 and did not have involvement with the operations post disposal. Therefore, under applicable accounting standards, the Company has classified its Media operations as discontinued operations for financial reporting purposes in all periods presented except where specifically identified otherwise.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
<BR>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	On March 19, 2015, the Company announced that it had entered into a non-binding letter of intent to sell the Media business to an unaffiliated third party. On July 1, 2015, the Company completed the sale of its Media business to&nbsp;Global Eagle Entertainment (&#147;GEE&#148;). Under the terms of the agreement, the Company sold $2,334 of customer receivables, property and equipment, and prepaid assets offset by $3,482 of assumed and transferred liabilities such as accounts payable, accrued revenue share and agency fees, and accrued liabilities of Media in exchange for cash. In addition, the transaction included certain amounts paid into escrow in full support of future potential obligations and an earn-out. The transaction resulted in a pre-tax gain of $2,340 and is presented in the Consolidated Statement of Comprehensive Loss. As part of the transaction agreement, GEE assumed all existing partner revenue sharing agreements and their related minimum revenue sharing requirements and certain vendor contracts held by Media. In addition, $854 of certain asset and lease impairment charges, severance expenses, and transaction costs were incurred as part of the transaction and are reflected in the net loss from discontinued operations. Since the facilities lease liabilities of the Media business were not assumed by GEE and will continue to be incurred under the existing contracts for their remaining terms without economic benefit, the Company has established cease-use dates for the facilities and recorded lease impairment liabilities based on the present value of the remaining future lease rentals, reduced by actual sublease rentals. This lease impairment liability of $498 is included in accrued liabilities of the Consolidated Balance Sheet at December 31, 2015. Also, some employees of Media were transferred to GEE as part of the transaction agreement. The terms of the escrow requires certain levels of performance related to a revenue sharing agreement and its related minimum revenue share requirements. &nbsp;In order for the Company to receive the earn-out payment, the buyer must successfully negotiate certain terms with a customer and the Media business must meet certain performance requirements over the 12 month period following the closing date.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
<BR>
</P>

<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
<B>
	17.&nbsp;Related Party Transactions
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
<BR>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	In August 2013, the Company entered into a two-year Management Services Agreement with 2012 DOOH Investments, LLC (the &quot;Consultant&quot;), an entity&nbsp;managed by Mr. Donald R. Wilson, a major stockholder. Under the agreement, the Consultant&nbsp;provides management consulting services to the Company and its subsidiaries with respect to financing, acquisitions, sourcing, diligence, and strategic planning.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
<BR>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	In consideration for its services, the Consultant received a one-time payment of 120,000 shares of the common stock of the Company which had a market value of $960 when issued in August 2013. The value of the common stock is amortized over the term of the agreement. The amortized expense charged to operations for the years ended December 31, 2015 and 2014 were $320 and $505, respectively. There was no unamortized value of the common stock after the third quarter of 2015. &nbsp;The unamortized value of the common stock was $320 at December 31, 2014 and was included in other current assets. Under the Agreement, the Consultant also received an annual services fee of $50, which terminated in July 2015.&nbsp;
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
<BR>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	The Company also had an agreement with a company owned by a board member under which it paid $15 a month for public relations services. This agreement was terminated on June 30, 2014. Under this agreement the Company incurred charges for the year ended December 31, 2014 of $90. The Company signed a new agreement with this company during 2015 under which it paid $10 a month for public relations services. Under this agreement, the Company has incurred charges of $121 for the year ended December 31, 2015.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
<BR>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	As discussed in Note 4, the Company&#146;s former senior lender sold its interest in the Company&#146;s Senior Credit Facility to a new lender group that included the Company&#146;s Executive Chairman and largest shareholder. Interest expense paid to the new lender group was $416 and $698 during the years ended December 31, 2015 and 2014, respectively.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
<BR>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
<B>
	18. Loss on Long-Term Contract
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
<BR>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	During the second quarter of 2014, the Company updated its analysis of a long-term partner related contract that originated in 2013. Based on the results of that analysis and an estimate of revenue to be generated in the future under the contract, the Company determined that sufficient revenue would not be generated under the contract for it to meet its minimum annual guarantees of revenue sharing to its partner.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
<BR>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=CENTER>
	63
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
<BR>
</P>
<HR STYLE="MARGIN-BOTTOM:9.6PX; PADDING-TOP:9.6PX" NOSHADE SIZE=1.333>
<A NAME="eolPage67"></A>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX; PAGE-BREAK-BEFORE:ALWAYS">
<BR>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	As a result, the Company recorded a $6,200 loss on the long-term contract at June 30, 2014, which represented the amount it expected that the total minimum annual guarantees payable to the partner would exceed the revenue generated under the contract at that time. The loss on the long-term contract was recorded as follows:
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	&nbsp;
</P>
<EFX_UNIDENTIFIED_TABLE>
<A NAME="FIS_UNIDENTIFIED_TABLE_36"></A>
<TABLE STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; FONT-SIZE:10PT" CELLPADDING=0 CELLSPACING=0 ALIGN=CENTER>
<TR HEIGHT=0 STYLE="FONT-SIZE:0">
<TD WIDTH=232 />
<TD WIDTH=25.467 />
<TD WIDTH=76.533 />
</TR>
<TR>
<TD STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; BACKGROUND-COLOR:#DBE5F1" VALIGN=TOP WIDTH=232>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	Loss on Long-Term Contract
</P>
</TD>
<TD STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; BACKGROUND-COLOR:#DBE5F1" VALIGN=BOTTOM WIDTH=25.467>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=RIGHT>
	$
</P>
</TD>
<TD STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; BACKGROUND-COLOR:#DBE5F1" VALIGN=BOTTOM WIDTH=76.533>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=RIGHT>
	4,130
</P>
</TD>
</TR>

	Total
</P>

<TD STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; BACKGROUND-COLOR:#DBE5F1" VALIGN=BOTTOM WIDTH=25.467>

	$

	6,200
</P>

<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
<BR>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	The Company continues to re-evaluate this loss contract status. During 2015, the Company reassessed its future revenue projections and operating costs for the remainder of the contract and made the decision to passively pursue revenue and operate the network with the minimum resources needed to maintain service levels as required by the agreement until it terminates on December 31, 2016. &nbsp;Based on this operating model, the Company revised its loss contract estimates during the year ended December 31, 2015, which resulted in a net gain of $444. &nbsp;At December 31, 2015 and 2014, the remaining balance on the loss on long-term contract was $616 and $3,685, respectively.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
<BR>

<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
<B>
	19. Subsequent Event
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
<BR>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	On March 9, 2016, the Company entered into the Second Amendment (the &#147;Second Amendment&#148;) to the Loan Agreement. The Second Amendment modifies, effective with the month ended February 2016, the minimum amounts of adjusted EBITDA that the Borrowers are required to maintain pursuant to a covenant contained in the Loan Agreement. Other than such change, the Second Amendment does not modify the terms of the Loan Agreement.
</P>

<DIV STYLE="WIDTH:720PX">
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=RIGHT>
<B>
	Exhibit 10.15
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=CENTER>
<B>
	FIRST AMENDMENT TO
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=CENTER>
<B>
	LOAN AND SECURITY AGREEMENT
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
<BR>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX">
<B>
	THIS FIRST AMENDMENT TO LOAN AND SECURITY AGREEMENT
</B>
	(this &#147;
<B>
	Amendment
</B>
	&#148;) is entered into effective as of November 17, 2015, by and among
<B>
	SILICON VALLEY BANK
</B>
	, a California corporation (&#147;
<B>
	Bank
</B>
	&#148;), and
<B>
	RMG NETWORKS HOLDING CORPORATION
</B>
	, a Delaware corporation,
<B>
	RMG NETWORKS, INC.
</B>
	, a Delaware corporation,
<B>
	RMG ENTERPRISE SOLUTIONS, INC.
</B>
	, a Delaware corporation,
<B>
	RMG NETWORKS LIMITED
</B>
	, a corporation formed under the laws of the United Kingdom, and
<B>
	RMG NETWORKS MIDDLE EAST, LLC
</B>
	, a Nevada limited liability company (collectively, &#147;
<B>
	Borrower
</B>
	&#148;). &nbsp;
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; FONT-SIZE:10PT" ALIGN=CENTER>
<B>
	RECITALS
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX; WIDTH:96PX; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	A.
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; TEXT-INDENT:-2PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	Bank and Borrower entered into that certain Loan and Security Agreement dated October 13, 2015 (as amended from time to time, the &#147;
<B>
	Loan Agreement
</B>
	&#148;).
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX; WIDTH:96PX; CLEAR:LEFT; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	B.
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; TEXT-INDENT:-2PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	Bank has extended credit to Borrower for the purposes permitted in the Loan Agreement. &nbsp;
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX; WIDTH:96PX; CLEAR:LEFT; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	C.
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; TEXT-INDENT:-2PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	Bank and Borrower have agreed to amend the definition of &#147;Borrowing Base&#148; to correct a scrivener&#146;s error.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; FONT-SIZE:10PT; CLEAR:LEFT" ALIGN=CENTER>
<B>
	AGREEMENT
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX; FONT-SIZE:10PT" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
<B>
	NOW, THEREFORE,
</B>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE:10PT">
	in consideration of the foregoing recitals and other good and valuable consideration, the receipt and adequacy of which is hereby acknowledged, and intending to be legally bound, the parties hereto agree as follows:
</FONT>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX; WIDTH:96PX; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	1.
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; PADDING-LEFT:0PX; TEXT-INDENT:-2PX">
<B>
	Definitions.
</B>
	&nbsp;Capitalized terms used but not defined in this Amendment shall have the meanings given to them in the Loan Agreement.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX; WIDTH:96PX; CLEAR:LEFT; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	2.
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; PADDING-LEFT:48PX; TEXT-INDENT:-2PX">
<B>
	Amendment to Loan Agreement
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:96PX; WIDTH:144PX; CLEAR:LEFT; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	2.1
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; TEXT-INDENT:-2PX">
<B>
	Definition of &#147;Borrowing Base&#148;. &nbsp;
</B>
	The definition of the term &#147;Borrowing Base&#148; set forth in Section 13.1 of the Loan Agreement is hereby amended and restated in its entirety as follows:
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX; PADDING-LEFT:96PX; PADDING-RIGHT:48PX; CLEAR:LEFT" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	&#147;
<B>
	Borrowing Base
</B>
	&#148; is the sum of (a) eighty percent (80%) of Eligible Accounts, plus (b) the lesser of (i) seventy percent (70%) of Eligible Foreign Accounts, or (ii) $500,000, all as determined by Bank from Borrower&#146;s most recent Transaction Report; provided, however, that Bank has the right to decrease the foregoing percentage in its good faith business judgment to mitigate the impact of events, conditions, contingencies, or risks which may adversely affect the Collateral or its value; any such change to be effective not earlier than five (5) Business Days following written notice by Bank to Borrower describing the reduction and reason(s) therefor. &nbsp;Notwithstanding the foregoing, Eligible Accounts due and owing to RMG Network Limited shall be excluded from the Borrowing Base until such time as the Debenture has been executed and Bank has a first priority, perfected security interest or other enforceable Lien in such Eligible Accounts under all applicable laws.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
<BR>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:96PX; WIDTH:144PX; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	2.2
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; TEXT-INDENT:-2PX">
<B>
	Limitation of Amendment. &nbsp;
</B>
	The amendment set forth in
<U>
	Section&nbsp;2.1
</U>
	, above, is effective for the purposes set forth herein and shall be limited precisely as written and shall not be deemed (a)&nbsp;to be a consent to any amendment, waiver or modification of any other term or condition of any Loan Document, or (b)&nbsp;to otherwise prejudice any right or remedy which Bank may now have or may have in the future under or in connection with any Loan Document.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX; WIDTH:96PX; CLEAR:LEFT; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	3.
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; PADDING-LEFT:0PX; TEXT-INDENT:-2PX">
<B>
	Counterparts.
</B>
	&nbsp;This Amendment may be executed in any number of counterparts and all of such counterparts taken together shall be deemed to constitute one and the same instrument.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX; WIDTH:96PX; CLEAR:LEFT; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	4.
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; PADDING-LEFT:0PX; TEXT-INDENT:-2PX">
<B>
	Effectiveness
</B>
	. &nbsp;This Amendment shall be effective upon the due execution and delivery to Bank of this Amendment by each party hereto.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX; WIDTH:96PX; CLEAR:LEFT; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	5.
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; PADDING-LEFT:0PX; TEXT-INDENT:-2PX">
<B>
	Binding Loan Agreement
</B>
	. &nbsp;This Amendment shall be binding upon, and shall inure to the benefit of, the parties&#146; respective representatives, successors and assigns.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX; WIDTH:96PX; CLEAR:LEFT; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	6.
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; PADDING-LEFT:0PX; TEXT-INDENT:-2PX">
<B>
	Further Assurances
</B>
	. &nbsp;The parties hereto shall execute such other documents as may be necessary or as may be required, in the opinion of counsel to Bank, to effect the transactions contemplated hereby and the liens and/or security interests of all other collateral instruments, as modified by this Amendment. &nbsp;Borrower also agrees to provide to Bank such other documents and instruments as Bank reasonably may request in connection with the modification effected hereby.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX; CLEAR:LEFT">
<BR>
<BR>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
	Page 1
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
<BR>
</P>
<HR STYLE="MARGIN-BOTTOM:9.6PX; PADDING-TOP:9.6PX" NOSHADE SIZE=1.333>
<A NAME="eolPage72"></A>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX; PAGE-BREAK-BEFORE:ALWAYS">
<BR>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX; WIDTH:96PX; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	7.
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; PADDING-LEFT:0PX; TEXT-INDENT:-2PX">
<B>
	Enforceability
</B>
	. &nbsp;In the event the enforceability or validity of any portion of this Amendment, the Loan Agreement or any of the other Loan Documents is challenged or questioned, such provision shall be construed in accordance with, and shall be governed by, whichever applicable federal law or law of the State of Texas would uphold or would enforce such challenged or questioned provision.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX; WIDTH:96PX; CLEAR:LEFT; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	8.
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; PADDING-LEFT:0PX; TEXT-INDENT:-2PX">
<B>
	Choice of Law
</B>
	. &nbsp;THIS AMENDMENT SHALL BE GOVERNED BY, AND CONSTRUED IN ACCORDANCE WITH, THE LAWS OF THE STATE OF TEXAS, EXCEPT TO THE EXTENT FEDERAL LAWS PREEMPT THE LAWS OF THE STATE OF TEXAS.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX; WIDTH:96PX; CLEAR:LEFT; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	9.
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; PADDING-LEFT:0PX; TEXT-INDENT:-2PX">
<B>
	Future Amendments
</B>
	. &nbsp;This Amendment and the other Loan Documents may be amended, revised, waived, discharged, released or terminated only by a written instrument or instruments, executed by the party against which enforcement of the amendment, revision, waiver, discharge, release or termination is asserted. &nbsp;Any alleged amendment, revision, waiver, discharge, release or termination which is not so documented shall not be effective as to any party.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX; CLEAR:LEFT" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	THIS AMENDMENT AND THE OTHER LOAN DOCUMENTS REPRESENT THE FINAL LOAN AGREEMENT BETWEEN THE PARTIES RELATED TO THE SUBJECT MATTER HEREIN CONTAINED AND MAY NOT BE CONTRADICTED BY EVIDENCE OF PRIOR, CONTEMPORANEOUS OR SUBSEQUENT ORAL AGREEMENTS OF THE PARTIES. &nbsp;THERE ARE NO UNWRITTEN ORAL AGREEMENTS BETWEEN THE PARTIES.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
<BR>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=CENTER>
	[Signature page follows.]

<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=CENTER>
<B>
	SECOND AMENDMENT TO
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=CENTER>
<B>
	LOAN AND SECURITY AGREEMENT
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
<BR>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX">
<B>
	THIS SECOND AMENDMENT TO LOAN AND SECURITY AGREEMENT
</B>
	(this &#147;
<B>
	Amendment
</B>
	&#148;) is entered into effective as of March 9, 2016, by and among
<B>
	SILICON VALLEY BANK
</B>
	, a California corporation (&#147;
<B>
	Bank
</B>
	&#148;), and
<B>
	RMG NETWORKS HOLDING CORPORATION
</B>
	, a Delaware corporation,

	RMG NETWORKS, INC.
</B>
	, a Delaware corporation,
<B>
	RMG ENTERPRISE SOLUTIONS, INC.
</B>
	, a Delaware corporation,
<B>
	RMG NETWORKS LIMITED
</B>
	, a corporation formed under the laws of the United Kingdom, and
<B>
	RMG NETWORKS MIDDLE EAST, LLC
</B>
	, a Nevada limited liability company (collectively, &#147;
<B>
	Borrower
</B>
	&#148;). &nbsp;
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN BOLD,TIMES NEW ROMAN" ALIGN=CENTER>
<B>
	RECITALS
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX; WIDTH:96PX; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	A.
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; TEXT-INDENT:-2PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	Bank and Borrower entered into that certain Loan and Security Agreement dated October 13, 2015 as amended by that certain First Amendment to Loan and Security Agreement dated November 17, 2015 (as may be further amended from time to time, the &#147;
<B>
	Loan Agreement
</B>
	&#148;).
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX; WIDTH:96PX; CLEAR:LEFT; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	B.
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; TEXT-INDENT:-2PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	Bank has extended credit to Borrower for the purposes permitted in the Loan Agreement. &nbsp;
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX; WIDTH:96PX; CLEAR:LEFT; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	C.
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; TEXT-INDENT:-2PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	Borrower has requested that Bank amend the Loan Agreement to revise the Minimum EBITDA financial covenant set forth in section 6.7 of the Loan Agreement.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX; WIDTH:96PX; CLEAR:LEFT; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	D.
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; TEXT-INDENT:-2PX" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
	Bank has agreed to so amend certain provisions of the Loan Agreement, but only to the extent, in accordance with the terms, subject to the conditions and in reliance upon the representations and warranties set forth below.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; FONT-FAMILY:TIMES NEW ROMAN BOLD,TIMES NEW ROMAN; CLEAR:LEFT" ALIGN=CENTER>
<B>
	AGREEMENT
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX; FONT-SIZE:6PT" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
<B>
	NOW, THEREFORE,
</B>
<FONT STYLE="FONT-SIZE:10PT">
	in consideration of the foregoing recitals and other good and valuable consideration, the receipt and adequacy of which is hereby acknowledged, and intending to be legally bound, the parties hereto agree as follows:
</FONT>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX; WIDTH:96PX; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	1.
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; PADDING-LEFT:0PX; TEXT-INDENT:-2PX">
<B>
	Definitions.
</B>
	&nbsp;Capitalized terms used but not defined in this Amendment shall have the meanings given to them in the Loan Agreement.
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:48PX; WIDTH:96PX; CLEAR:LEFT; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	2.
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:11.133PX; PADDING-LEFT:48PX; TEXT-INDENT:-2PX">
<B>
	Amendment to Loan Agreement
</B>
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:96PX; WIDTH:144PX; CLEAR:LEFT; FLOAT:LEFT">
<B>
	2.1
</B>
</P>

</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; MARGIN-BOTTOM:-2PX; TEXT-INDENT:96PX; WIDTH:144PX; CLEAR:LEFT; FLOAT:LEFT">
	(a)

<U>
	EBITDA
</U>
	. &nbsp;&nbsp;As measured as of the end of each fiscal month as indicated below for the three (3) month period then ending, EBITDA, plus the amount of (a) non-cash stock compensation expense, (b) non-cash warrant adjustments, (c) non-cash gain or loss from discontinued operations, and (d) non-cash long term contract adjustments, each as determined by Bank, of at least the following:
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX; CLEAR:LEFT" ALIGN=JUSTIFY>
<BR>
</P>

</B>
	. &nbsp;The parties hereto shall execute such other documents as may be necessary or as may be required, in the opinion of counsel to Bank, to effect the transactions contemplated hereby and the liens and/or security interests of all other collateral instruments, as modified by this Amendment. &nbsp;Borrower also agrees to provide to Bank such other documents and instruments as Bank reasonably may request in connection with the modification effected hereby.
</P>

</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX" ALIGN=CENTER>

</B>

<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
	I, Robert Michelson, certify that:
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX; TEXT-INDENT:33.733PX">
	1.&nbsp; &nbsp;I have reviewed this annual report on Form 10-K of RMG Networks Holding Corporation;
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX; TEXT-INDENT:33.733PX">
	2.&nbsp;&nbsp; Based on my knowledge, this report does not contain any untrue statement of a material fact or omit to state a material fact necessary to make the statements made, in light of the circumstances under which such statements were made, not misleading with respect to the period covered by this report;
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX; TEXT-INDENT:33.733PX">
	3.&nbsp;&nbsp; Based on my knowledge, the financial statements, and other financial information included in this report, fairly present in all material respects the financial condition, results of operations and cash flows of the registrant as of, and for, the periods presented in this report;
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX; TEXT-INDENT:33.733PX">
	4.&nbsp;&nbsp; The registrant&#146;s other certifying officer and I are responsible for establishing and maintaining disclosure controls and procedures (as defined in Exchange Act Rules&nbsp;13a-15(e) and 15d-15(e)) and internal control over financial reporting (as defined in Exchange Act Rules 13a-15(f) and 15d-15(f)) for the registrant and have:
</P>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
	&nbsp;
</P>
<TABLE STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX; FONT-SIZE:10PT" CELLPADDING=0 CELLSPACING=0>

	a)
</P>
</TD>
<TD STYLE="MARGIN-TOP:0PX" VALIGN=TOP WIDTH=657.6>
<P STYLE="MARGIN:0PX">
	designed such disclosure controls and procedures, or caused such disclosure controls and procedures to be designed under our supervision, to ensure that material information relating to the registrant, including its consolidated subsidiaries, is made known to us by others within those entities, particularly during the period in which this report is being prepared;
</P>
</TD>
